# Character Mode — Roster Sprites (Pokémon Emerald Seaglass v3.0)

Each character's **final-evolution** roster with sprites (regional/cosmetic forms shown as base species). Sprites via [PokéAPI](https://github.com/PokeAPI/sprites). Text version: `ROSTERS.md`.

> ⚠️ **Work in progress** — rosters not final.

**170 characters.**

## Contents
- [Generation 1](#generation-1)
- [Generation 2](#generation-2)
- [Generation 3](#generation-3)
- [Generation 4](#generation-4)
- [Generation 5](#generation-5)
- [Generation 6](#generation-6)
- [Generation 7](#generation-7)
- [Generation 8](#generation-8)
- [Generation 9](#generation-9)
